bballdave025@MY_MACHINE /cygdrive/c/David/FHTW-2025-All_-_move_2024_get_new/Classified_-_Almost_Just_3lett_FS_-_Combined
$ cat >/dev/null <<'EOF'
>
>
##########################################################################
########    MULTIPLE CLASSES stuff #
#+ For any directory (the directory with everything sorted or any of the
#+ single directories), get all the `mcl` entries. (point the 0th)
#+ With the underscores and legal classifications. PROBABLY DO ` | wc -l`
$ find . -type f -iname "*.jpg" | \
    awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' | \
      grep -io "\(_\(abg\|cwa\|fko\|fmr\|gni\|iac\|mbr\|mcl\|"\
"mmx\|nbr\|oic\|orc\|scg\|spr\|suh\|tbr\|ucr\)\)\+[.]jpg$" | \
      sed 's#[.]jpg$##g' | \
        grep "mcl"
#+ These should all either:
#+   1. Have one and only one yes-binary-model classification, 'f25m3'.
#+      in which case there should not be an 'mbr'
#+ # FIND ANY WITH MORE THAN ONE CLASSIFICATION (and no 'mbr') (BAD)
 $ find . -type f -iname "*.jpg" | \
     awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' | \
       grep -io "\(_\(abg\|cwa\|fko\|fmr\|gni\|iac\|mbr\|mcl\|"\
"mmx\|nbr\|oic\|orc\|scg\|spr\|suh\|tbr\|ucr\)\)\+[.]jpg$" | \
       sed 's#[.]jpg$##g' | \
         grep "mcl" | grep -v "mbr" |
           grep -P '(?<!_(cwa|fmr|gni|nbr|orc|scg|spr|tbr|ucr))'\
'(cwa|fmr|gni|nbr|orc|scg|spr|tbr|ucr)'\
'(?=_(cwa|fmr|gni|nbr|orc|scg|spr|tbr|ucr))'
>
> EOF

>
> mcl stuff continued.
>
> $ #
 #  FIND THE ONE AND ONLY ONE SINGLE CLASSIFICATION
 #+ (with no 'mbr') (GOOD)
 $ find . -type f -iname "*.jpg" | \
     awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' | \
       grep -io "\(_\(abg\|cwa\|fko\|fmr\|gni\|iac\|mbr\|mcl\|"\
"mmx\|nbr\|oic\|orc\|scg\|spr\|suh\|tbr\|ucr\)\)\+[.]jpg$" | \
       sed 's#[.]jpg$##g' | \
         grep "mcl" | grep -v "mbr" |

'_(cwa|fmr|gni|nbr|orc|scg|spr|tbr|ucr)'\
'(?!_(cwa|fmr|gni|nbr|orc|scg|spr|tbr|ucr))'

 $ # FIND THOSE WITHOUT ACCOMPANYING SINGLE (and no 'mbr') (BAD)
 $ find . -type f -iname "*.jpg" | \
     awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' | \

"mmx\|nbr\|oic\|orc\|scg\|spr\|suh\|tbr\|ucr\)\)\+[.]jpg$" | \
       sed 's#[.]jpg$##g' | \

         grep -v "\(cwa\|fmr\|gni\|nbr\|orc\|scg\|spr\|tbr\|ucr\)"
#+   2. Have 'mbr' and more than one yes-binary-model classification.
>
> EOF

$ cfcf

######### COMMANDS CAN BE COPY/PASTED, OR YOU CAN USE THE IDEAS #########
######### TO GET WHAT YOU WANT. (DON'T INCLUDE LEADING $S)      #########

$ #
#  USE THIS MOST - combined for characters, non-ascii;
#+ and characters, non-printable ascii--includes space,
#+ tab, carriage return, linefeed
# @@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@ IMPORTANT CHECK 1 @@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@
$ find . -type f | awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' |
    LC_ALL=C grep -oP "[\x00-\x20\x7F-\xFF]" | wc -l
$ # @@@@@@@@@
$ ##### Possible subsets if desired #####
$ ##      - Any with non-printable ASCII (definitely control chars)
    $ find . -type f | awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' |
        LC_ALL=C grep -oP "[\x00-\x08\x0B-\x0C\x0E-\x1F\x7F]" | wc -l
$ #
#  Any with undesired space-y (still 'printable' in that they show
#+ up, but control-y), tab, line feed, carriage return, space
#+ ( I don't include:
#+        VERTICAL TAB  -  \x0B , \013 ;
#+   or   FORM FEED     -  \x0C , \014 ;
#+   I guess they're technically in the same group, but I don't
#+   run into them nearly as often, so I put them in the
#+   general control character group.)
    $ find . -type f | awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' |
        LC_ALL=C grep -oP "[\x09-\x10\x0B\x0D\x20]" | wc -l
$ ##### Any that are actually non-ASCII? #####
    $ find . -type f | awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' |
        Do LC_ALL=C grep -oP "[\x80-\xFF]" | wc -l
$ #  Do LC_ALL=C we have any filenames with undesired
$ #+ ASCII characters (Dave's no-nos)
$ # So, to find out if any filenames have those unwanted characters
$ # @@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@ IMPORTANT CHECK 2 @@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@
$ find . -type f | awk -F'/' '{print $NF}' |
    LC_ALL=C grep '[] ~!@#$%^&|\/)(}{[*?><;:"`'"'"']' | wc -l
$ # @@@@@@@@@

#  This is as good a place as any to put these next notes, which
#+ are useful for fixing the new replay cleaning of runscript results
#+ Note to WATCH OUT for false positives when joining lines that
#+ got cut by the right side of the terminal.
#+ The right-side-of-the-terminal thing is why we have a series of
#+ regexes having multiples of 80. If the terminal width has been
#+ changed, the regexes will need to change in order to match the
#+ width. The width can be found with   tput cols
## (Cleaning still not perfect, but better now than before. I'm pretty
#+ sure the problem is specific to Cygwin but haven't tested.)
#
#  The series of regexes is specifically for Notepad++ and has a few
#+ quirks specific to that program. There shouldn't be any spaces.

   Srch:   ^(.{80})\n(.+)$      Repl:   \1\2
   Srch:   ^(.{160})\n(.+)$     Repl:   \1\2

# and so forth with 240, 320, ... if needed.

#########################################################################

$ do_check=1 && change_count=0 &&
while IFS= read line; do
  this_str="${line}"
  if [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})(.+$) ]]; then
    beg=${BASH_REMATCH[1]} spaces=${BASH_REMATCH[2]} end=${BASH_REMATCH[3]}
    len_beg="${#beg}" len_spaces="${#spaces}" len_end="${#end}"
    echo
    echo "# FOR CHECKING #"
    echo "len_beg: ${len_beg} len_spaces: ${len_spaces} len_end: ${len_end}"
    is_a_match=0
    test $(echo "$len_beg + $len_spaces" | bc) -eq 80 && is_a_match=1
    if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]; then
      change_count=$(echo "${change_count}+1" | bc)
      echo "  CHANGE"
      echo "${this_str}"
      echo "  TO"
      echo "${first}"
      echo "${last}"
    fi ##endof:  if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]
  fi ##endof:  if <bash_rematch match>
done < /cygdrive/c/David/my_repos_dwb/fhtw-paper-code-prep/dataset_preparation_examples/terminal_logfile_woes.log

$ do_check=1 && change_count=0 &&
while IFS= read line; do
  this_str="${line}"
  if [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})(.+$) ]]; then
    beg=${BASH_REMATCH[1]} spaces=${BASH_REMATCH[2]} end=${BASH_REMATCH[3]}
    len_beg="${#beg}" len_spaces="${#spaces}" len_end="${#end}"
    echo
    if [ $do_check ]; then
      echo "# FOR CHECKING #"
      echo -n "len_beg: ${len_beg} "
      echo -n "len_spaces: ${len_spaces} "
      echo    "len_end: ${len_end}"
    fi ##endof: if [ $do_check ]
    is_a_match=0  # guilty until proven innocent
    test $(( ($len_beg + $len_spaces) % 80 )) -eq 0 && is_a_match=1
    if [ $is_a_match ]; then
      change_count=$(echo "${change_count}+1" | bc)
      echo "  CHANGE"
      echo "${this_str}"
      echo "  TO"
      echo "${beg}"
      echo "${end}"
    fi ##endof:  if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]
  fi ##endof:  if <bash_rematch regex matches>
done < /cygdrive/c/David/my_repos_dwb/fhtw-paper-code-prep/dataset_preparation_examples/terminal_logfile_woes.log

test $change_count -eq 0 && echo "No matches. No changes needed."

$ find_spaces_not_linefeed() {
  use="Usage:\n% find_spaces_not_linefeed LOGFILENAME "\
"[TERMINAL_WIDTH] [DO_CHECK_FOR_LENGTH]"
 if [ $# -eq 0 ]; then
  echo -e "Name of/path to logfile required\n${usage}"
 fi
 if [ $# -ge 1 ]; then input_logfile_name=$1; fi
 terminal_width=80
 if [ $# -ge 2 ]; then terminal_width=$2; fi
 do_check=0
 if [ $# -ge 3 ]; then do_check=$3; fi
 change_count=0
 while IFS= read line; do
  this_str="${line}"
  if [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})(.+$) ]]; then
    beg=${BASH_REMATCH[1]} spaces=${BASH_REMATCH[2]} end=${BASH_REMATCH[3]}
    len_beg="${#beg}" len_spaces="${#spaces}" len_end="${#end}"
    if [ $do_check ]; then
      echo
      echo "# FOR CHECKING #"
      echo -n "len_beg: ${len_beg} "
      echo -n "len_spaces: ${len_spaces} "
      echo    "len_end: ${len_end}"
    fi ##endof: if [ $do_check ]
    is_a_match=0  # guilty until proven innocent
    test $(( ($len_beg + $len_spaces) % 80 )) -eq 0 && is_a_match=1
    if [ $is_a_match ]; then
      change_count=$(echo "${change_count}+1" | bc)
      if [ ! $do_check ]; then echo; fi
      echo "  CHANGE"
      echo "${this_str}"
      echo "  TO"
      echo "${beg}"  # Will put in a linefeed between the two
      echo "${end}"
    fi ##endof:  if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]
  fi ##endof:  if <bash_rematch regex matches>
 done < "${input_logfile_name}"
 test $change_count -eq 0 && echo "No matches. No changes needed."
} ##endof:  find_spaces_not_linefeed

$ find_spaces_not_linefeed() {
  use="Usage:\n% find_spaces_not_linefeed LOGFILENAME "\
"[TERMINAL_WIDTH] [DO_CHECK_FOR_LENGTH]"
  if [ $# -eq 0 ]; then
    echo -e "Name of/path to logfile required\n${usage}"
  fi
  if [ $# -ge 1 ]; then input_logfile_name=$1; fi
  terminal_width=80
  if [ $# -ge 2 ]; then terminal_width=$2; fi
  do_check=0
  if [ $# -ge 3 ]; then do_check=$3; fi
  change_count=0
  while IFS= read line; do
    this_str="${line}"
    if [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})(.+$) ]]; then
      beg=${BASH_REMATCH[1]} spaces=${BASH_REMATCH[2]} end=${BASH_REMATCH[3]}
      len_beg="${#beg}" len_spaces="${#spaces}" len_end="${#end}"
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo
        echo "# FOR CHECKING #"
        echo -n "len_beg: ${len_beg} "
        echo -n "len_spaces: ${len_spaces} "
        echo    "len_end: ${len_end}"
      fi ##endof: if [ $do_check -ne 0 ] #<1>
      is_a_match=0  # guilty until proven innocent
      test_value=$(( ($len_beg + $len_spaces) % 80 ))
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo "To be tested:"
        echo "test_value: ${test_value}"
      fi ##endof:  if [ $do_check -ne 0 ] #<2>
      test ${test_value} -eq 0 && is_a_match=1
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo "is_a_match: ${is_a_match}"
      fi ##endof: if [ $do_check -ne 0 ] #<3>
      if [ $is_a_match ]; then
        change_count=$(echo "${change_count}+1" | bc)
        if [ $do_check -eq 0 ]; then echo; fi
        echo "  CHANGE"
        echo "${this_str}"
        echo "  TO"
        echo "${beg}"  # Will put in a linefeed between the two
        echo "${end}"
        echo "  WITH a linefeed and not spaces."
      fi ##endof:  if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]
    fi ##endof:  if <bash_rematch regex matches>
  done < "${input_logfile_name}"
  test $change_count -eq 0 && echo "No matches. No changes needed."
} ##endof:  find_spaces_not_linefeed

$ find_spaces_not_linefeed() {
  use="Usage:\n% find_spaces_not_linefeed LOGFILENAME "\
"[TERMINAL_WIDTH] [DO_CHECK_FOR_LENGTH]"
  if [ $# -eq 0 ]; then
    echo -e "Name of/path to logfile required\n${usage}"
  fi
  if [ $# -ge 1 ]; then input_logfile_name=$1; fi
  terminal_width=80
  if [ $# -ge 2 ]; then terminal_width=$2; fi
  do_check=0
  if [ $# -ge 3 ]; then do_check=$3; fi
  change_count=0
  while IFS= read line; do
    this_str="${line}"
    if [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})(.+$) ]]; then
      beg=${BASH_REMATCH[1]} spaces=${BASH_REMATCH[2]} end=${BASH_REMATCH[3]}
      len_beg="${#beg}" len_spaces="${#spaces}" len_end="${#end}"
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo
        echo "# FOR CHECKING #"
        echo -n "len_beg: ${len_beg} "
        echo -n "len_spaces: ${len_spaces} "
        echo    "len_end: ${len_end}"
      fi ##endof: if [ $do_check -ne 0 ] #<1>
      is_a_match=0  # guilty until proven innocent
      test_value=$(( ($len_beg + $len_spaces) % 80 ))
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo "To be tested:"
        echo "test_value: ${test_value}"
      fi ##endof:  if [ $do_check -ne 0 ] #<2>
      test ${test_value} -eq 0 && is_a_match=1
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo "is_a_match: ${is_a_match}"
      fi ##endof: if [ $do_check -ne 0 ] #<3>
      if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]; then
        change_count=$(echo "${change_count}+1" | bc)
        if [ $do_check -eq 0 ]; then echo; fi
        echo "  CHANGE"
        echo "${this_str}"
        echo "  TO"
        echo "${beg}"  # Will put in a linefeed between the two
        echo "${end}"
        echo "##WITH a linefeed and not spaces."
      fi ##endof:  if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]
    fi ##endof:  if <bash_rematch regex matches>
  done < "${input_logfile_name}"
  test $change_count -eq 0 && echo "No matches. No changes needed."
} ##endof:  find_spaces_not_linefeed

$ find_spaces_not_linefeed() {
  use="Usage:\n% find_spaces_not_linefeed LOGFILENAME "\
"[TERMINAL_WIDTH] [DO_CHECK_FOR_LENGTH]"
  if [ $# -eq 0 ]; then
    echo -e "Name of/path to logfile required\n${usage}"
  fi
  if [ $# -ge 1 ]; then input_logfile_name=$1; fi
  terminal_width=80; if [ $# -ge 2 ]; then terminal_width=$2; fi
  do_check=0
  if [ $# -ge 3 ]; then do_check=$3; fi
  change_count=0
  while IFS= read line; do
    this_str="${line}"
    # Another useful alternative, depending on details, is
    #  [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})([^ ].*$) ]]
    if [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})(.+$) ]]; then
      beg=${BASH_REMATCH[1]} spaces=${BASH_REMATCH[2]} end=${BASH_REMATCH[3]}
      len_beg="${#beg}" len_spaces="${#spaces}" len_end="${#end}"
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo; echo "# FOR CHECKING #"; echo -n "len_beg: ${len_beg} "
        echo -n "len_spaces: ${len_spaces} "; echo "len_end: ${len_end}"
      fi ##endof: if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]
      is_a_match=0  # guilty until proven innocent
      test_value=$(( ($len_beg + $len_spaces) % 80 ))
      test ${test_value} -eq 0 && is_a_match=1
      if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]; then
        change_count=$(echo "${change_count}+1" | bc)
        if [ $do_check -eq 0 ]; then echo; fi
        echo "  CHANGE"
        echo "${this_str}"
        echo "  TO"
        echo "${beg}"  # Will put in a linefeed between the two
        echo "${end}"
        echo "##### WITH a linefeed and not spaces."
      fi ##endof:  if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]
    fi ##endof:  if <bash_rematch regex matches>
  done < "${input_logfile_name}"
  test $change_count -eq 0 && echo "No matches. No changes needed."
} ##endof:  find_spaces_not_linefeed

$ find_spaces_not_linefeed() {
  use="Usage:\n% find_spaces_not_linefeed LOG [WIDTH] [DO_CHECK_LENGTH]"
  if [ $# -eq 0 ]; then echo -e "Path to logfile required\n${usage}"; fi
  if [ $# -ge 1 ]; then input_logfile_name=$1; fi
  terminal_width=80; if [ $# -ge 2 ]; then terminal_width=$2; fi
  do_check=0; if [ $# -ge 3 ]; then do_check=$3; fi
  change_count=0
  while IFS= read line; do
    this_str="${line}"
    if [[ $this_str =~ (^.+)([ ]{10,})([^ ].*$) ]]; then
      beg=${BASH_REMATCH[1]} spaces=${BASH_REMATCH[2]} end=${BASH_REMATCH[3]}
      len_beg="${#beg}" len_spaces="${#spaces}" len_end="${#end}"
      if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]; then
        echo; echo "# FOR CHECKING #"; echo -n "len_beg: ${len_beg} "
        echo -n "len_spaces: ${len_spaces} "; echo "len_end: ${len_end}"
      fi ##endof: if [ $do_check -ne 0 ]
      is_a_match=0  # guilty until proven innocent
      test_value=$(( ($len_beg + $len_spaces) % 80 ))
      test ${test_value} -eq 0 && is_a_match=1
      if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]; then
        change_count=$(echo "${change_count}+1" | bc)
        if [ $do_check -eq 0 ]; then echo; fi
        echo "  CHANGE"; echo "${this_str}"; echo "  TO"
        echo "${beg}"  # Will put in a linefeed between the two
        echo "${end}"
        echo "##### WITH a linefeed and not spaces."
      fi ##endof:  if [ $is_a_match -eq 1 ]
    fi ##endof:  if <bash_rematch regex matches>
  done < "${input_logfile_name}"
  test $change_count -eq 0 && echo "No matches found. No changes needed."
} ##endof:  find_spaces_not_linefeed

bballdave025@MY_MACHINE /cygdrive/c/David/FHTW-2025-All_-_move_2024_get_new/Classified_-_Almost_Just_3lett_FS_-_Combined
$ type windowsphotoviewer
windowsphotoviewer is a function
windowsphotoviewer ()
{
    IFS='
' read -r -d '' usage <<'End_WPV_Usage'
.

NAME
       windowsphotoviewer - opens the Notepad++ in background
       Often invoked with aliases including
         winphoto, wpv

SYNOPSIS
       windowsphotoviewer [--help|-h] FILENAME

DESCRIPTION
       Usable on Cygwin (running in Windows 10), assuming that
       its filepath is
        `/cygdrive/c/Program\ Files/Windows\ Photo\ Viewer/PhotoViewer.dll'
       a.k.a.
        `"C:\\Program Files\\Windows Photo Viewer\\PhotoViewer.dll"'

       Opens the file, FILENAME in Windows Photo Viewer, which program
       opens in the background via `rundll32'.

       First argument(s)
         Unless passed `--help' or `-h' as the first argument,
         the argument is tested for its existence as a file,
         and then Windows Photo Viewer will attempt to open
         it if the results are positive, and the return code
         will be `0'. (This means that any problems concerning
         compatibility of the file and WPV will be handled by
         WPV, and Cygwin won't know anything about it.) If the
         string given doesn't represent an existing filename,
         the function exits to the shell with return code, `1'.
         If no FILENAME parameter is given, the function exits
         to the shell with return code, `2'.

         If I find I need it, I will extend this to where all
         arguments are opened (if they represent existing files),
         rather than just ignoring arguments $2, $3, $4. In the
         meanwhile, I'll just output something saying that $1
         (argument outputted) will be opened and the rest of the
         arguments (outputted as well) will be ignored, after
         which this usage string will be outputted, after which
         the first argument will be opened in Notepad++ (again,
         as long as `--help' or `-h' is given as the first
         argument). The return code will be `0'.

         If `--help' or `-h' is given as the first argument,
         this usage will be outputted, and the program will
         give return code `0'

AUTHOR
         David BLACK,   GitHub  @bballdave025
         @since 2025-08-12.

Note for dev. Working command from Cygwin was (where I entered
it as one line)

powershell -c '
rundll32
  "C:\Program Files\Windows Photo Viewer\PhotoViewer.dll",
    ImageView_Fullscreen
      "C:\David\FHTW-2025-All_-_move_2024_get_new\"\
"Classified_-_Almost_Just_3lett_FS_-_Combined\Tiny_Background_Reuse\"\
"BeineckeMs1119-10622001_00114_tbr.jpg"' &

.
End_WPV_Usage

    this_arg=$1
    this_param=;
    this_used_param=;
    retval=0;
    shift;
    if [ "${this_arg}" = "--help" -o "${this_arg}" = "-h" ]; then
        echo "${usage}" | sed 's#^[.]$##g' 1>&2;
        return ${retval};
    else
        this_param="${this_arg}";
        this_pre_param=$(realpath "${this_param}");
        this_used_param=$(cygpath -w "${this_param}");
        if [ ${#@} -gt 0 ]; then
            echo " Extra parameters:" 1>&2;
            echo "$@" 1>&2;
            echo " will be ignored." 1>&2;
        fi;
        if [ ! -z "${this_used_param}" ]; then
            if [ -f "${this_used_param}" ]; then
                echo " Attempting to open" 1>&2;
                echo "${this_used_param}" 1>&2;
                echo " in Windows Photo Viewer" 1>&2;
            else
                echo " Your parameter," 1>&2;
                echo "${this_used_param}" 1>&2;
                echo " is not a file." 1>&2;
                echo " Note that the file path from here is" 1>&2;
                echo "${this_used_param}" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo "${usage}" | sed 's#^[.]$##g' 1>&2;
                retval=1;
            fi;
        else
            echo " You must call the function with a FILENAME parameter" 1>&2;
            retval=2;
        fi;
    fi;
    if [ ${retval} -eq 0 ]; then
        powershell -c '
      rundll32 "C:\Program Files\Windows Photo Viewer\PhotoViewer.dll",
                      ImageView_Fullscreen '\"${this_used_param}\"'
    ' &
    fi;
    return ${retval}
}

$ type windowsphotoviewer
windowsphotoviewer is a function
windowsphotoviewer ()
{
    this_arg=$1;
    this_param=;
    this_used_param=;
    retval=0;
    shift;
    if [ "${this_arg}" = "--help" -o "${this_arg}" = "-h" ]; then
        echo "${usage}" | sed 's#^[.]$##g' 1>&2;
        return ${retval};
    else
        this_param="${this_arg}";
        this_pre_param=$(realpath "${this_param}");
        this_used_param=$(cygpath -w "${this_pre_param}");
        if [ ${#@} -gt 0 ]; then
            echo " Extra parameters:" 1>&2;
            echo "$@" 1>&2;
            echo " will be ignored." 1>&2;
        fi;
        if [ ! -z "${this_used_param}" ]; then
            if [ -f "${this_used_param}" ]; then
                echo " Attempting to open" 1>&2;
                echo "${this_used_param}" 1>&2;
                echo " in Windows Photo Viewer" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo " YOU SHOULD SEE something (but with numbers) like" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo "----------" 1>&2;
                echo "[f] ghij" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo "me@MACHINE /current/working/dir" 1>&2;
                echo "\$ # HIT [ENTER] HERE, maybe a few times" 1>&2;
                echo "  # AFTER CLICKING BACK TO CYGWIN." 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo " YOU SHOULD THEN SEE something like" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo "[2]+  Done                    powershell -c '" 1>&2;
                echo "      rundll32  PhotoViewer  parameter" 1>&2;
                echo "    '" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo "me@MACHINE /current/working/dir" 1>&2;
                echo "\$" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo " TRUST ME!";
                echo " DOING SO WILL LIKELY RESOLVE SOME CONFUSION." 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo " CLICK HERE, THEN PRESS [ENTER] A FEW TIMES." 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo "----------" 1>&2;
            else
                echo " Your parameter," 1>&2;
                echo "${this_used_param}" 1>&2;
                echo " is not a file." 1>&2;
                echo " Note that the full file path is" 1>&2;
                echo "${this_used_param}" 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo 1>&2;
                echo "${usage}" | sed 's#^[.]$##g' 1>&2;
                retval=1;
            fi;
        else
            echo " You must call the function with a FILENAME parameter" 1>&2;
            retval=2;
        fi;
    fi
}
